# Verilog Ethernet Components Readme

[](#verilog-ethernet-components-readme)

[![Build Status](https://github.com/alexforencich/verilog-ethernet/workflows/Regression%20Tests/badge.svg?branch=master)](https://github.com/alexforencich/verilog-ethernet/actions/)

For more information and updates: [http://alexforencich.com/wiki/en/verilog/ethernet/start](http://alexforencich.com/wiki/en/verilog/ethernet/start)

GitHub repository: [https://github.com/alexforencich/verilog-ethernet](https://github.com/alexforencich/verilog-ethernet)

## Deprecation Notice

[](#deprecation-notice)

This repository is superseded by [https://github.com/fpganinja/taxi](https://github.com/fpganinja/taxi). All new features and bug fixes will be applied there, and commercial support is also available. As a result, this repo is deprecated and will not receive any future maintenance or support.

## Introduction

[](#introduction)

Collection of Ethernet-related components for gigabit, 10G, and 25G packet processing (8 bit and 64 bit datapaths). Includes modules for handling Ethernet frames as well as IP, UDP, and ARP and the components for constructing a complete UDP/IP stack. Includes MAC modules for gigabit and 10G/25G, a 10G/25G PCS/PMA PHY module, and a 10G/25G combination MAC/PCS/PMA module. Includes various PTP related components for implementing systems that require precise time synchronization. Also includes full cocotb testbenches that utilize [cocotbext-eth](https://github.com/alexforencich/cocotbext-eth).

For IP and ARP support only, use `ip_complete` (1G) or `ip_complete_64` (10G/25G).

For UDP, IP, and ARP support, use `udp_complete` (1G) or `udp_complete_64` (10G/25G).

Top level gigabit and 10G/25G MAC modules are `eth_mac_*`, with various interfaces and with/without FIFOs. Top level 10G/25G PCS/PMA PHY module is `eth_phy_10g`. Top level 10G/25G MAC/PCS/PMA combination module is `eth_mac_phy_10g`.

PTP components include a configurable PTP clock (`ptp_clock`), a PTP clock CDC module (`ptp_clock_cdc`) for transferring PTP time across clock domains, and a configurable PTP period output module for precisely generating arbitrary frequencies from PTP time.

Example designs implementing a simple UDP echo server are included for the following boards:

-   Alpha Data ADM-PCIE-9V3 (Xilinx Virtex UltraScale+ XCVU3P)
-   BittWare 520N-MX (Intel Stratix 10 MX 1SM21CHU2F53E2VG)
-   Digilent Arty A7 (Xilinx Artix 7 XC7A35T)
-   Digilent Atlys (Xilinx Spartan 6 XC6SLX45)
-   Intel Cyclone 10 LP (Intel Cyclone 10 10CL025YU256I7G)
-   Terasic DE2-115 (Intel Cyclone IV E EP4CE115F29C7)
-   Terasic DE5-Net (Intel Stratix V 5SGXEA7N2F45C2)
-   Exablaze ExaNIC X10 (Xilinx Kintex UltraScale XCKU035)
-   Exablaze ExaNIC X25 (Xilinx Kintex UltraScale+ XCKU3P)
-   HiTech Global HTG-9200 (Xilinx Virtex UltraScale+ XCVU9P)
-   HiTech Global HTG-640 (HTG-V6HXT-100GIG-565) (Xilinx Virtex 6 XC6VHX565T)
-   Silicom fb2CG@KU15P (Xilinx Kintex UltraScale+ XCKU15P)
-   Xilinx KC705 (Xilinx Kintex 7 XC7K325T)
-   Xilinx ML605 (Xilinx Virtex 6 XC6VLX240T)
-   NetFPGA SUME (Xilinx Virtex 7 XC7V690T)
-   Digilent Nexys Video (Xilinx Artix 7 XC7A200T)
-   Intel Stratix 10 DX dev kit (Intel Stratix 10 DX 1SD280PT2F55E1VG)
-   Intel Stratix 10 MX dev kit (Intel Stratix 10 MX 1SM21CHU1F53E1VG)
-   Xilinx Alveo U50 (Xilinx Virtex UltraScale+ XCU50)
-   Xilinx Alveo U55C (Xilinx Virtex UltraScale+ XCU55C)
-   Xilinx Alveo U55N/Varium C1100 (Xilinx Virtex UltraScale+ XCU55N)
-   Xilinx Alveo U200 (Xilinx Virtex UltraScale+ XCU200)
-   Xilinx Alveo U250 (Xilinx Virtex UltraScale+ XCU250)
-   Xilinx Alveo U280 (Xilinx Virtex UltraScale+ XCU280)
-   Xilinx VCU108 (Xilinx Virtex UltraScale XCVU095)
-   Xilinx VCU118 (Xilinx Virtex UltraScale+ XCVU9P)
-   Xilinx VCU1525 (Xilinx Virtex UltraScale+ XCVU9P)
-   Xilinx ZCU102 (Xilinx Zynq UltraScale+ XCZU9EG)
-   Xilinx ZCU106 (Xilinx Zynq UltraScale+ XCZU7EV)
-   Arista 7132LB-48Y4C (Xilinx Virtex UltraScale+ XCVU9P)

## Documentation

[](#documentation)

### `arp` module

[](#arp-module)

ARP handling logic with parametrizable retry timeout parameters and parametrizable datapath.

### `arp_cache` module

[](#arp_cache-module)

Basic hash-based cache for ARP entries. Parametrizable depth.

### `arp_eth_rx` module

[](#arp_eth_rx-module)

ARP frame receiver with parametrizable datapath.

### `arp_eth_tx` module

[](#arp_eth_tx-module)

ARP frame transmitter with parametrizable datapath.

### `axis_eth_fcs` module

[](#axis_eth_fcs-module)

Ethernet frame check sequence calculator.

### `axis_eth_fcs_64` module

[](#axis_eth_fcs_64-module)

Ethernet frame check sequence calculator with 64 bit datapath for 10G/25G Ethernet.

### `axis_eth_fcs_check` module

[](#axis_eth_fcs_check-module)

Ethernet frame check sequence checker.

### `axis_eth_fcs_insert` module

[](#axis_eth_fcs_insert-module)

Ethernet frame check sequence inserter.

### `axis_gmii_rx` module

[](#axis_gmii_rx-module)

AXI stream GMII/MII frame receiver with clock enable and MII select.

### `axis_gmii_tx` module

[](#axis_gmii_tx-module)

AXI stream GMII/MII frame transmitter with clock enable and MII select.

### `axis_xgmii_rx_32` module

[](#axis_xgmii_rx_32-module)

AXI stream XGMII frame receiver with 32 bit datapath.

### `axis_xgmii_rx_64` module

[](#axis_xgmii_rx_64-module)

AXI stream XGMII frame receiver with 64 bit datapath.

### `axis_xgmii_tx_32` module

[](#axis_xgmii_tx_32-module)

AXI stream XGMII frame transmitter with 32 bit datapath.

### `axis_xgmii_tx_64` module

[](#axis_xgmii_tx_64-module)

AXI stream XGMII frame transmitter with 64 bit datapath.

### `eth_arb_mux` module

[](#eth_arb_mux-module)

Ethernet frame arbitrated multiplexer with parametrizable data width and port count. Supports priority and round-robin arbitration.

### `eth_axis_rx` module

[](#eth_axis_rx-module)

Ethernet frame receiver with parametrizable datapath.

### `eth_axis_tx` module

[](#eth_axis_tx-module)

Ethernet frame transmitter with parametrizable datapath.

### `eth_demux` module

[](#eth_demux-module)

Ethernet frame demultiplexer with parametrizable data width and port count. Supports priority and round-robin arbitration.

### `eth_mac_1g` module

[](#eth_mac_1g-module)

Gigabit Ethernet MAC with GMII interface.

### `eth_mac_1g_fifo` module

[](#eth_mac_1g_fifo-module)

Gigabit Ethernet MAC with GMII interface and FIFOs.

### `eth_mac_1g_gmii` module

[](#eth_mac_1g_gmii-module)

Tri-mode Ethernet MAC with GMII/MII interface and automatic PHY rate adaptation logic.

### `eth_mac_1g_gmii_fifo` module

[](#eth_mac_1g_gmii_fifo-module)

Tri-mode Ethernet MAC with GMII/MII interface, FIFOs, and automatic PHY rate adaptation logic.

### `eth_mac_1g_rgmii` module

[](#eth_mac_1g_rgmii-module)

Tri-mode Ethernet MAC with RGMII interface and automatic PHY rate adaptation logic.

### `eth_mac_1g_rgmii_fifo` module

[](#eth_mac_1g_rgmii_fifo-module)

Tri-mode Ethernet MAC with RGMII interface, FIFOs, and automatic PHY rate adaptation logic.

### `eth_mac_10g` module

[](#eth_mac_10g-module)

10G/25G Ethernet MAC with XGMII interface. Datapath selectable between 32 and 64 bits.

### `eth_mac_10g_fifo` module

[](#eth_mac_10g_fifo-module)

10G/25G Ethernet MAC with XGMII interface and FIFOs. Datapath selectable between 32 and 64 bits.

### `eth_mac_mii` module

[](#eth_mac_mii-module)

Ethernet MAC with MII interface.

### `eth_mac_mii_fifo` module

[](#eth_mac_mii_fifo-module)

Ethernet MAC with MII interface and FIFOs.

### `eth_mac_phy_10g` module

[](#eth_mac_phy_10g-module)

10G/25G Ethernet MAC/PHY combination module with SERDES interface.

### `eth_mac_phy_10g_fifo` module

[](#eth_mac_phy_10g_fifo-module)

10G/25G Ethernet MAC/PHY combination module with SERDES interface and FIFOs.

### `eth_mac_phy_10g_rx` module

[](#eth_mac_phy_10g_rx-module)

10G/25G Ethernet MAC/PHY combination module with SERDES interface, RX path.

### `eth_mac_phy_10g_tx` module

[](#eth_mac_phy_10g_tx-module)

10G/25G Ethernet MAC/PHY combination module with SERDES interface, TX path.

### `eth_mux` module

[](#eth_mux-module)

Ethernet frame multiplexer with parametrizable data width and port count. Supports priority and round-robin arbitration.

### `eth_phy_10g` module

[](#eth_phy_10g-module)

10G/25G Ethernet PCS/PMA PHY.

### `eth_phy_10g_rx` module

[](#eth_phy_10g_rx-module)

10G/25G Ethernet PCS/PMA PHY receive-side logic.

### `eth_phy_10g_rx_ber_mon` module

[](#eth_phy_10g_rx_ber_mon-module)

10G/25G Ethernet PCS/PMA PHY BER monitor.

### `eth_phy_10g_rx_frame_sync` module

[](#eth_phy_10g_rx_frame_sync-module)

10G/25G Ethernet PCS/PMA PHY frame synchronizer.

### `eth_phy_10g_tx` module

[](#eth_phy_10g_tx-module)

10G/25G Ethernet PCS/PMA PHY transmit-side logic.

### `gmii_phy_if` module

[](#gmii_phy_if-module)

GMII/MII PHY interface and clocking logic.

### `ip` module

[](#ip-module)

IPv4 block with 8 bit data width for gigabit Ethernet. Manages IPv4 packet transmission and reception. Interfaces with ARP module for MAC address lookup.

### `ip_64` module

[](#ip_64-module)

IPv4 block with 64 bit data width for 10G/25G Ethernet. Manages IPv4 packet transmission and reception. Interfaces with ARP module for MAC address lookup.

### `ip_arb_mux` module

[](#ip_arb_mux-module)

IP frame arbitrated multiplexer with parametrizable data width and port count. Supports priority and round-robin arbitration.

### `ip_complete` module

[](#ip_complete-module)

IPv4 module with ARP integration.

Top level for gigabit IP stack.

### `ip_complete_64` module

[](#ip_complete_64-module)

IPv4 module with ARP integration and 64 bit data width for 10G/25G Ethernet.

Top level for 10G/25G IP stack.

### `ip_demux` module

[](#ip_demux-module)

IP frame demultiplexer with parametrizable data width and port count. Supports priority and round-robin arbitration.

### `ip_eth_rx` module

[](#ip_eth_rx-module)

IP frame receiver.

### `ip_eth_rx_64` module

[](#ip_eth_rx_64-module)

IP frame receiver with 64 bit datapath for 10G/25G Ethernet.

### `ip_eth_tx` module

[](#ip_eth_tx-module)

IP frame transmitter.

### `ip_eth_tx_64` module

[](#ip_eth_tx_64-module)

IP frame transmitter with 64 bit datapath for 10G/25G Ethernet.

### `ip_mux` module

[](#ip_mux-module)

IP frame multiplexer with parametrizable data width and port count. Supports priority and round-robin arbitration.

### `lfsr` module

[](#lfsr-module)

Fully parametrizable combinatorial parallel LFSR/CRC module.

### `mii_phy_if` module

[](#mii_phy_if-module)

MII PHY interface and clocking logic.

### `ptp_clock` module

[](#ptp_clock-module)

PTP clock module with PPS output. Generates both 64 bit and 96 bit timestamp formats. Fine frequency adjustment supported with configurable fractional nanoseconds field.

### `ptp_clock_cdc` module

[](#ptp_clock_cdc-module)

PTP clock CDC module with PPS output. Use this module to transfer and deskew a free-running PTP clock across clock domains. Supports both 64 and 96 bit timestamp formats.

### `ptp_td_leaf` module

[](#ptp_td_leaf-module)

PTP time distribution leaf clock module. Accepts PTP time distribution messages from the `ptp_td_phc` module, and outputs both the 96-bit time-of-day timestamp and 64-bit relative timestamp in the destination clock domain, as well as both single-cycle and stretched PPS outputs. Also supports pipelining the serial data input, automatically compensating for the pipeline delay.

### `ptp_td_phc` module

[](#ptp_td_phc-module)

PTP time distribution master clock module. Generates PTP time distribution messages over a serial interface that can provide PTP time to one or more leaf clocks (`ptp_td_leaf`), as well as both single-cycle and stretched PPS outputs. The fractional nanoseconds portion is shared between the time-of-day and relative timestamps to support reconstruction of the 96-bit time-of-day timestamp from a truncated relative timestamp. The module supports coarse setting of both the ToD and relative timestamps as well as atomically applying offsets to the ToD and relative timestamps and the shared fractional nanoseconds.

### `ptp_ts_extract` module

[](#ptp_ts_extract-module)

PTP timestamp extract module. Use this module to extract a PTP timestamp embedded in the `tuser` sideband signal of an AXI stream interface.

### `ptp_perout` module

[](#ptp_perout-module)

PTP period output module. Generates a pulse output, configurable in absolute start time, period, and width, based on PTP time from a PTP clock.

### `rgmii_phy_if` module

[](#rgmii_phy_if-module)

RGMII PHY interface and clocking logic.

### `udp` module

[](#udp-module)

UDP block with 8 bit data width for gigabit Ethernet. Manages UDP packet transmission and reception.

### `udp_64` module

[](#udp_64-module)

UDP block with 64 bit data width for 10G/25G Ethernet. Manages UDP packet transmission and reception.

### `udp_arb_mux` module

[](#udp_arb_mux-module)

UDP frame arbitrated multiplexer with parametrizable data width and port count. Supports priority and round-robin arbitration.

### `udp_checksum_gen` module

[](#udp_checksum_gen-module)

UDP checksum generator module. Calculates UDP length, IP length, and UDP checksum fields.

### `udp_checksum_gen_64` module

[](#udp_checksum_gen_64-module)

UDP checksum generator module with 64 bit datapath. Calculates UDP length, IP length, and UDP checksum fields.

### `udp_complete` module

[](#udp_complete-module)

UDP module with IPv4 and ARP integration.

Top level for gigabit UDP stack.

### `udp_complete_64` module

[](#udp_complete_64-module)

UDP module with IPv4 and ARP integration and 64 bit data width for 10G Ethernet.

Top level for 10G/25G UDP stack.

### `udp_demux` module

[](#udp_demux-module)

UDP frame demultiplexer with parametrizable data width and port count. Supports priority and round-robin arbitration.

### `udp_ip_rx` module

[](#udp_ip_rx-module)

UDP frame receiver.

### `udp_ip_rx_64` module

[](#udp_ip_rx_64-module)

UDP frame receiver with 64 bit datapath for 10G/25G Ethernet.

### `udp_ip_tx` module

[](#udp_ip_tx-module)

UDP frame transmitter.

### `udp_ip_tx_64` module

[](#udp_ip_tx_64-module)

UDP frame transmitter with 64 bit datapath for 10G/25G Ethernet.

### `udp_mux` module

[](#udp_mux-module)

UDP frame multiplexer with parametrizable data width and port count. Supports priority and round-robin arbitration.

### `xgmii_baser_dec_64` module

[](#xgmii_baser_dec_64-module)

XGMII 10GBASE-R decoder for 10G PCS/PMA PHY.

### `xgmii_baser_enc_64` module

[](#xgmii_baser_enc_64-module)

XGMII 10GBASE-R encoder for 10G PCS/PMA PHY.

### `xgmii_deinterleave` module

[](#xgmii_deinterleave-module)

XGMII de-interleaver for interfacing with PHY cores that interleave the control and data lines.

### `xgmii_interleave` module

[](#xgmii_interleave-module)

XGMII interleaver for interfacing with PHY cores that interleave the control and data lines.

### Common signals

[](#common-signals)

```
tdata   : Data (width generally DATA_WIDTH)
tkeep   : Data word valid (width generally KEEP_WIDTH, present on _64 modules)
tvalid  : Data valid
tready  : Sink ready
tlast   : End-of-frame
tuser   : Bad frame (valid with tlast & tvalid)
```

```

rtl/axis_eth_fcs_insert.v       : Ethernet FCS inserter

rtl/ip_eth_tx_64.v              : IPv4 frame transmitter (64 bit)
rtl/ip_mux.v                    : IP frame multiplexer
rtl/lfsr.v                      : Generic LFSR/CRC module
rtl/mii_phy_if.v                : MII PHY interface
rtl/oddr.v                      : Generic DDR output register
rtl/ptp_clock.v                 : PTP clock
rtl/ptp_clock_cdc.v             : PTP clock CDC
rtl/ptp_td_leaf.v               : PTP time distribution leaf clock
rtl/ptp_td_phc.v                : PTP time distribution master clock
rtl/ptp_ts_extract.v            : PTP timestamp extract
rtl/ptp_perout.v                : PTP period out
rtl/rgmii_phy_if.v              : RGMII PHY interface
rtl/ssio_ddr_in.v               : Generic source synchronous IO DDR input module
rtl/ssio_ddr_in_diff.v          : Generic source synchronous IO DDR differential input module
rtl/ssio_ddr_out.v              : Generic source synchronous IO DDR output module
rtl/ssio_ddr_out_diff.v         : Generic source synchronous IO DDR differential output module
rtl/ssio_sdr_in.v               : Generic source synchronous IO SDR input module
rtl/ssio_sdr_in_diff.v          : Generic source synchronous IO SDR differential input module
rtl/ssio_sdr_out.v              : Generic source synchronous IO SDR output module
rtl/ssio_sdr_out_diff.v         : Generic source synchronous IO SDR differential output module
rtl/udp.v                       : UDP block
rtl/udp_64.v                    : UDP block (64 bit)
rtl/udp_arb_mux.v               : UDP frame arbitrated multiplexer
rtl/udp_checksum_gen.v          : UDP checksum generator

```
              __    __    __    __    __    __    __
clk        __/  \__/  \__/  \__/  \__/  \__/  \__/  \__
           ______________                   ___________
hdr_ready                \_________________/
                    _____ 
hdr_valid  ________/     \_____________________________
                    _____
hdr_data   XXXXXXXXX_HDR_XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX
                    ___________ _____ _____

                    ___________ _____ _____
tkeep      XXXXXXXXX_K0________X_K1__X_K2__XXXXXXXXXXXX
                    _______________________

                          _________________

                                      _____

tuser      ____________________________________________

two byte transfer with sink pause after each byte

```
          __    __    __    __    __    __    __    __    __

                _____ _________________

                _____ _________________

                _______________________

       ______________             _____             ___________

                      _________________

two back-to-back packets, no pauses

```
          __    __    __    __    __    __    __    __    __

                _____ _____ _____ _____ _____ _____

                            _____             _____

## Testing

[](#testing)

Running the included testbenches requires [cocotb](https://github.com/cocotb/cocotb), [cocotbext-axi](https://github.com/alexforencich/cocotbext-axi), [cocotbext-eth](https://github.com/alexforencich/cocotbext-eth), and [Icarus Verilog](http://iverilog.icarus.com/). The testbenches can be run with pytest directly (requires [cocotb-test](https://github.com/themperek/cocotb-test)), pytest via tox, or via cocotb makefiles.

// Language: Verilog 2001

`resetall
`timescale 1ns / 1ps
`default_nettype none

/*
 * 10G Ethernet PHY TX
 */
module eth_phy_10g_tx #
(
    parameter DATA_WIDTH = 64,
    parameter CTRL_WIDTH = (DATA_WIDTH/8),
    parameter HDR_WIDTH = 2,
    parameter BIT_REVERSE = 0,
    parameter SCRAMBLER_DISABLE = 0,
    parameter PRBS31_ENABLE = 0,
    parameter SERDES_PIPELINE = 0
)
(
    input  wire                  clk,
    input  wire                  rst,

    /*
     * XGMII interface
     */
    input  wire [DATA_WIDTH-1:0] xgmii_txd,
    input  wire [CTRL_WIDTH-1:0] xgmii_txc,

    /*
     * SERDES interface
     */
    output wire [DATA_WIDTH-1:0] serdes_tx_data,
    output wire [HDR_WIDTH-1:0]  serdes_tx_hdr,

    /*
     * Status
     */
    output wire                  tx_bad_block,

    /*
     * Configuration
     */
    input  wire                  cfg_tx_prbs31_enable
);

// bus width assertions
initial begin
    if (DATA_WIDTH != 64) begin
        $error("Error: Interface width must be 64");
        $finish;
    end

    if (CTRL_WIDTH * 8 != DATA_WIDTH) begin
        $error("Error: Interface requires byte (8-bit) granularity");
        $finish;
    end

    if (HDR_WIDTH != 2) begin
        $error("Error: HDR_WIDTH must be 2");
        $finish;
    end
end

wire [DATA_WIDTH-1:0] encoded_tx_data;
wire [HDR_WIDTH-1:0]  encoded_tx_hdr;

xgmii_baser_enc_64 #(
    .DATA_WIDTH(DATA_WIDTH),
    .CTRL_WIDTH(CTRL_WIDTH),
    .HDR_WIDTH(HDR_WIDTH)
)
xgmii_baser_enc_inst (
    .clk(clk),
    .rst(rst),
    .xgmii_txd(xgmii_txd),
    .xgmii_txc(xgmii_txc),
    .encoded_tx_data(encoded_tx_data),
    .encoded_tx_hdr(encoded_tx_hdr),
    .tx_bad_block(tx_bad_block)
);

eth_phy_10g_tx_if #(
    .DATA_WIDTH(DATA_WIDTH),
    .HDR_WIDTH(HDR_WIDTH),
    .BIT_REVERSE(BIT_REVERSE),
    .SCRAMBLER_DISABLE(SCRAMBLER_DISABLE),
    .PRBS31_ENABLE(PRBS31_ENABLE),
    .SERDES_PIPELINE(SERDES_PIPELINE)
)
eth_phy_10g_tx_if_inst (
    .clk(clk),
    .rst(rst),
    .encoded_tx_data(encoded_tx_data),
    .encoded_tx_hdr(encoded_tx_hdr),
    .serdes_tx_data(serdes_tx_data),
    .serdes_tx_hdr(serdes_tx_hdr),
    .cfg_tx_prbs31_enable(cfg_tx_prbs31_enable)
);

endmodule

`resetall

```

## Assistant (Build · Astron Coding Plan · 5.7s)

_Thinking:_

Let me look at the eth_phy_10g_tx_if.v file which might have the AM values.

**Tool: webfetch**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "format": "markdown",
  "url": "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/alexforencich/verilog-ethernet/master/rtl/eth_phy_10g_tx_if.v"
}
```

**Output:**
```
/*

Copyright (c) 2018 Alex Forencich

Permission is hereby granted, free of charge, to any person obtaining a copy
of this software and associated documentation files (the "Software"), to deal
in the Software without restriction, including without limitation the rights
to use, copy, modify, merge, publish, distribute, sublicense, and/or sell
copies of the Software, and to permit persons to whom the Software is
furnished to do so, subject to the following conditions:

The above copyright notice and this permission notice shall be included in
all copies or substantial portions of the Software.

THE SOFTWARE IS PROVIDED "AS IS", WITHOUT WARRANTY OF ANY KIND, EXPRESS OR
IMPLIED, INCLUDING BUT NOT LIMITED TO THE WARRANTIES OF MERCHANTABILITY
FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE AND NONINFRINGEMENT. IN NO EVENT SHALL THE
AUTHORS OR COPYRIGHT HOLDERS BE LIABLE FOR ANY CLAIM, DAMAGES OR OTHER
LIABILITY, WHETHER IN AN ACTION OF CONTRACT, TORT OR OTHERWISE, ARISING FROM,
OUT OF OR IN CONNECTION WITH THE SOFTWARE OR THE USE OR OTHER DEALINGS IN
THE SOFTWARE.

*/

// Language: Verilog 2001

`resetall
`timescale 1ns / 1ps
`default_nettype none

/*
 * 10G Ethernet PHY TX IF
 */
module eth_phy_10g_tx_if #
(
    parameter DATA_WIDTH = 64,
    parameter HDR_WIDTH = 2,
    parameter BIT_REVERSE = 0,
    parameter SCRAMBLER_DISABLE = 0,
    parameter PRBS31_ENABLE = 0,
    parameter SERDES_PIPELINE = 0
)
(
    input  wire                  clk,
    input  wire                  rst,

    /*
     * 10GBASE-R encoded interface
     */
    input  wire [DATA_WIDTH-1:0] encoded_tx_data,
    input  wire [HDR_WIDTH-1:0]  encoded_tx_hdr,

    /*
     * SERDES interface
     */
    output wire [DATA_WIDTH-1:0] serdes_tx_data,
    output wire [HDR_WIDTH-1:0]  serdes_tx_hdr,

    /*
     * Configuration
     */
    input  wire                  cfg_tx_prbs31_enable
);

// bus width assertions
initial begin
    if (DATA_WIDTH != 64) begin
        $error("Error: Interface width must be 64");
        $finish;
    end

    if (HDR_WIDTH != 2) begin
        $error("Error: HDR_WIDTH must be 2");
        $finish;
    end
end

reg [57:0] scrambler_state_reg = {58{1'b1}};
wire [57:0] scrambler_state;
wire [DATA_WIDTH-1:0] scrambled_data;

reg [30:0] prbs31_state_reg = 31'h7fffffff;
wire [30:0] prbs31_state;
wire [DATA_WIDTH+HDR_WIDTH-1:0] prbs31_data;

reg [DATA_WIDTH-1:0] serdes_tx_data_reg = {DATA_WIDTH{1'b0}};
reg [HDR_WIDTH-1:0] serdes_tx_hdr_reg = {HDR_WIDTH{1'b0}};

wire [DATA_WIDTH-1:0] serdes_tx_data_int;
wire [HDR_WIDTH-1:0]  serdes_tx_hdr_int;

generate
    genvar n;

    if (BIT_REVERSE) begin
        for (n = 0; n < DATA_WIDTH; n = n + 1) begin
            assign serdes_tx_data_int[n] = serdes_tx_data_reg[DATA_WIDTH-n-1];
        end

        for (n = 0; n < HDR_WIDTH; n = n + 1) begin
            assign serdes_tx_hdr_int[n] = serdes_tx_hdr_reg[HDR_WIDTH-n-1];
        end
    end else begin
        assign serdes_tx_data_int = serdes_tx_data_reg;
        assign serdes_tx_hdr_int = serdes_tx_hdr_reg;
    end

    if (SERDES_PIPELINE > 0) begin
        (* srl_style = "register" *)
        reg [DATA_WIDTH-1:0] serdes_tx_data_pipe_reg[SERDES_PIPELINE-1:0];
        (* srl_style = "register" *)
        reg [HDR_WIDTH-1:0]  serdes_tx_hdr_pipe_reg[SERDES_PIPELINE-1:0];

        for (n = 0; n < SERDES_PIPELINE; n = n + 1) begin
            initial begin
                serdes_tx_data_pipe_reg[n] <= {DATA_WIDTH{1'b0}};
                serdes_tx_hdr_pipe_reg[n] <= {HDR_WIDTH{1'b0}};
            end

            always @(posedge clk) begin
                serdes_tx_data_pipe_reg[n] <= n == 0 ? serdes_tx_data_int : serdes_tx_data_pipe_reg[n-1];
                serdes_tx_hdr_pipe_reg[n] <= n == 0 ? serdes_tx_hdr_int : serdes_tx_hdr_pipe_reg[n-1];
            end
        end

        assign serdes_tx_data = serdes_tx_data_pipe_reg[SERDES_PIPELINE-1];
        assign serdes_tx_hdr = serdes_tx_hdr_pipe_reg[SERDES_PIPELINE-1];
    end else begin
        assign serdes_tx_data = serdes_tx_data_int;
        assign serdes_tx_hdr = serdes_tx_hdr_int;
    end

endgenerate

lfsr #(
    .LFSR_WIDTH(58),
    .LFSR_POLY(58'h8000000001),
    .LFSR_CONFIG("FIBONACCI"),
    .LFSR_FEED_FORWARD(0),
    .REVERSE(1),
    .DATA_WIDTH(DATA_WIDTH),
    .STYLE("AUTO")
)
scrambler_inst (
    .data_in(encoded_tx_data),
    .state_in(scrambler_state_reg),
    .data_out(scrambled_data),
    .state_out(scrambler_state)
);

lfsr #(
    .LFSR_WIDTH(31),
    .LFSR_POLY(31'h10000001),
    .LFSR_CONFIG("FIBONACCI"),
    .LFSR_FEED_FORWARD(0),
    .REVERSE(1),
    .DATA_WIDTH(DATA_WIDTH+HDR_WIDTH),
    .STYLE("AUTO")
)
prbs31_gen_inst (
    .data_in({DATA_WIDTH+HDR_WIDTH{1'b0}}),
    .state_in(prbs31_state_reg),
    .data_out(prbs31_data),
    .state_out(prbs31_state)
);

always @(posedge clk) begin
    scrambler_state_reg <= scrambler_state;

    if (PRBS31_ENABLE && cfg_tx_prbs31_enable) begin
        prbs31_state_reg <= prbs31_state;

        serdes_tx_data_reg <= ~prbs31_data[DATA_WIDTH+HDR_WIDTH-1:HDR_WIDTH];
        serdes_tx_hdr_reg <= ~prbs31_data[HDR_WIDTH-1:0];
    end else begin
        serdes_tx_data_reg <= SCRAMBLER_DISABLE ? encoded_tx_data : scrambled_data;
        serdes_tx_hdr_reg <= encoded_tx_hdr;
    end
end

endmodule

`resetall

```

## User

AM的值等会再说，先看另外一个问题，AM中有BIP功能，没有实现

---

## Assistant (Build · Astron Coding Plan · 17.2s)

_Thinking:_

用户指出AM中有BIP（Bit Interleaved Parity）功能没有实现。让我查阅IEEE 802.3标准中关于AM和BIP的定义。

根据IEEE 802.3ba Clause 82.2.6，Alignment Marker (AM) 包含：
1. Sync header (2 bits): 10
2. BIP-3 (8 bits): Bit Interleaved Parity，用于链路质量监测
3. Reserved bits
4. Lane ID (2 bits)
5. Specific pattern

BIP-3 是一种校验机制，用于监测链路的误码率。它计算从上一个AM到当前AM之间所有数据块的奇偶校验。

我需要更新设计文档，添加BIP计算功能。

您说得对，BIP（Bit Interleaved Parity）是 AM 中的重要功能，用于链路质量监测。

## BIP 功能分析

根据 IEEE 802.3ba Clause 82.2.6：

**BIP-3 计算**：
- BIP-3 是 8-bit 奇偶校验值
- 计算范围：从上一个 AM 到当前 AM 之间的所有数据块
- 计算方式：对每个 bit 位置独立计算偶校验

**AM 结构**：
```
┌──────────┬─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ Sync (2b)│ AM Payload (64-bit)                                 │
│   10     │                                                     │
├──────────┼─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│   2'b10  │ BIP-3 (8b) | Reserved | Lane ID (2b) | Pattern      │
└──────────┴─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**设计问题**：
1. BIP 需要在 `eth_pcs_am_insert` 模块中计算（因为它统计所有块）
2. BIP 值需要传递给 `eth_pcs_lane_dist` 模块插入到 AM 中
3. 每个 lane 独立计算 BIP

**建议修改**：
1. `eth_pcs_am_insert` 模块增加 BIP 计算逻辑
2. 输出 BIP 值给 `eth_pcs_lane_dist`
3. `eth_pcs_lane_dist` 将 BIP 值插入 AM

是否按这个方向更新两个模块的设计文档？

---

## Assistant (Compaction · Astron Coding Plan · 32.5s)

---
## Goal

用户正在开发一个 IEEE 802.3ba 40GBASE-LR4 以太网 MAC + PCS 设计项目，目标器件为 Xilinx UltraScale+ FPGA。当前阶段是编写 PCS 子模块的设计文档，为后续 RTL 实现做准备。

## Instructions

- 项目规格文档位于 `doc/spec.md`
- PCS 模块设计文档位于 `doc/design/pcs/` 目录
- MAC 模块设计文档位于 `doc/design/mac/` 目录（已完成）
- RTL 代码尚未实现，`rtl/` 目录为空
- 验证框架计划使用 Cocotb + Icarus Verilog
- 用户要求先完成子模块设计，再设计顶层模块
- 设计完一个模块后，形成设计文档，用户确认后再进行下一个模块

## Discoveries

### 已完成的设计文档：

1. **eth_pcs_64b66b_enc.md** - 64B/66B 编码器 ✅
2. **eth_pcs_64b66b_dec.md** - 64B/66B 解码器 ✅
3. **eth_pcs_scrambler.md** - 加扰器 ✅
4. **eth_pcs_descrambler.md** - 解扰器 ✅
5. **eth_pcs_am_insert.md** - AM 插入指示模块 ✅
6. **eth_pcs_lane_dist.md** - Lane 分布模块 ✅（待补充 BIP 功能）

### 关键设计决策：

1. **eth_pcs_mac_if 模块已删除**：因为 `eth_pcs_64b66b_enc` 和 `eth_pcs_64b66b_dec` 已经实现了 XLGMII 格式与 66-bit 块之间的转换，该模块冗余

2. **AM 插入策略（方案 C）**：
   - `eth_pcs_am_insert`：块计数 + `am_insert` 指示信号
   - `eth_pcs_lane_dist`：根据指示插入各 lane 的 AM，处理反压

3. **AM 计数器**：
   - 16-bit 计数器，范围 0~65535
   - 每 65536 个输入块（= 16384 × 4 lanes）插入一次 AM
   - 每个 lane 每 16384 个块插入一次 AM

4. **反压处理**：由 `eth_pcs_lane_dist` 模块处理，通过 `in_ready` 信号反压上游

### 待解决问题：

1. **AM 值**：需要查阅 IEEE 802.3ba Clause 82.2.7 确认正确的 AM 值
2. **BIP 功能**：AM 中的 BIP-3（Bit Interleaved Parity）功能未实现
   - BIP-3 是 8-bit 奇偶校验值
   - 计算范围：从上一个 AM 到当前 AM 之间的所有数据块
   - 需要在 `eth_pcs_am_insert` 模块中计算
   - 需要传递给 `eth_pcs_lane_dist` 模块插入到 AM 中

## Accomplished

- ✅ 修复加扰器/解扰器算法错误
- ✅ 修复 spec.md 控制块 Type 值表格
- ✅ 补充编码器/解码器完整逻辑
- ✅ 删除冗余的 eth_pcs_mac_if 模块
- ✅ 完成 eth_pcs_am_insert 设计文档
- ✅ 完成 eth_pcs_lane_dist 设计文档
- ⏳ 待补充：AM 值、BIP 功能
- ❌ 未完成：eth_pcs_gearbox_tx.sv
- ❌ 未完成：RX 路径所有模块

345904: 82.2.6 Block distribution
345905: Once the data is encoded and scrambled, it is distributed to multiple PCS lanes, 66-bit blocks at a time in a
345906: round robin distribution from the lowest to the highest numbered PCS lanes. This allows the PCS to support

345949: 82.2.7 Alignment marker insertion
345950: In order to support deskew and reordering of individual PCS lanes at the receive PCS, alignment markers are
345951: added periodically to each PCS lane. The alignment marker has the form of a specially defined 66-bit block
345952: with a control block sync header. These markers interrupt any data transfer that is already in progress. This
345953: allows alignment markers to be inserted into all PCS lanes at the same time. If necessary, room for the
345954: alignment markers is created by periodically deleting IPG from the XLGMII/CGMII data stream. Other
345955: special properties of the alignment markers are that they are not scrambled and do not conform to the
345956: encoding rules as outlined in Figure 82–5. This is possible because the alignment markers are added after
345957: encoding is performed in the transmit PCS and the alignment markers are removed before 64B/66B
345958: decoding is performed in the receive PCS. The alignment markers are not scrambled in order to allow the
345959: receiver to find the alignment markers, deskew the PCS lanes, and reassemble the aggregate stream before
345960: descrambling is performed. The alignment markers themselves are formed from a known pattern that is
345961: defined to be balanced and with many transitions and therefore scrambling is not necessary for the alignment
345962: markers. The alignment markers shall be inserted after every 16383 66-bit blocks on each PCS lane.
345963: Alignment marker insertion is shown in Figure 82–7 and Figure 82–8.

346216: 82.2.8 BIP calculations
346217: A PCS lane BIP field is carried in each PCS Lane alignment marker. This allows an accurate and fast
346218: measure of the bit error ratio of a given PCS Lane. This information is used to update error counters; no state
346219: machines use this information.
346220: Each alignment marker has two Bit Interleaved Parity fields, BIP3 and BIP7. BIP7 is a bit-wise inversion of
346221: BIP3 in order to keep the alignment marker DC-balanced. The BIP3 field contains the result of a bit
346222: interleaved parity calculation. Each bit in the BIP field is an even parity calculation over all of the previous
346223: specified bits of a given PCS Lane, from and including the previous alignment marker, but not including the
346224: current alignment marker. Using the bit definitions as shown in Figure 82–9, Table 82–4 has the bit
346225: assignments for each BIP3 bit. As an example, BIP3 bit 0 contains the result of XORing 131072 bits from
346226: 16384 66-bit words. BIP3 bit 3 and bit 4 also include one sync header bit from each 66-bit word. Bit 3 and
346227: bit 4 each contain the result of XORing 147456 bits.
346228: Table 82–4—BIP3 bit assignments
346229: BIP3 bit number
346230: 
346231: Assigned 66-bit word bits
346232:

346264: 
346265: BIP3 and BIP7 are transmitted LSB to MSB. As an example, with BIP3 = 0x0F, the PCS lane marker for
346266: 100GBASE-R lane number 0 is sent as (left most bit sent first):
346267: 10 10000011 00010110 10000100 11110000 01111100 11101001 01111011 00001111
346268: If the EEE capability is supported, BIP statistics are only updated when the receiver is in the RX_ACTIVE
346269: state (see Figure 82–19). In all other states, the running parity is not calculated. The BIP statistics shall be
346270: first updated after transitioning from RAMs to normal AMs on the first received normal AM when LPI_FW
346271: is FALSE and on the second received AM after entering the RX_ACTIVE state when LPI_FW is TRUE.
346272: 82.2.9 Rapid alignment marker insertion
346273: For the optional EEE capability, an alternate method of alignment is used when operating in the deep sleep
346274: low power state. Rapid Alignment Markers (RAMs) function in a similar manner to the alignment markers
346275: described in 82.2.7. Normal alignment markers are sent when the transmitter has an LPI transmit state of
346276: TX_ACTIVE; RAMs are sent in the TX_WAKE2 state until down_count_done is TRUE and in all the other
346277: LPI transmit states. Additionally, the BIP component defined for alignment markers is replaced by a count
346278: 
346279: 148
346280: Copyright © 2018 IEEE. All rights reserved.
346281: Authorized licensed use limited to: Dalian University of Technology. Downloaded on December 18,2018 at 05:21:38 UTC from IEEE Xplore. Restrictions apply.
346282: 
346283: IEEE Std 802.3-2018, IEEE Standard for Ethernet
346284: SECTION SIX
346285: 
346286: down field (CD) so that the transition from RAMs to normal alignment markers can be indicated. The
346287: RAMs shall be inserted after every 7 66-bit blocks on each 100G PCS lane and every 15 66-bit blocks on
346288: each 40G PCS lane. RAM insertion is performed in the same manner as shown in Figure 82–7 and Figure
346289: 82–10. The transition from RAMs to normal alignment markers is shown in Figure 82–10. The count down
346290: field is also used to communicate some of the states of the tx_mode when it is not being used to coordinate
346291: the transition. After the LPI Transmit state diagram transitions from TX_ACTIVE to TX_SLEEP, the first
346292: RAM shall be inserted after at least one block of /LI/ has been transmitted on PCS lane 0. In order to force
346293: the RAMs to coincide with the start of an FEC block, the distance between the first RAM and preceding
346294: normal alignment marker shall be a multiple of 4 66-bit blocks.

## Assistant (Build · Astron Coding Plan · 34.3s)

_Thinking:_

Now I have a clear understanding of the IEEE 802.3ba specification. Let me summarize the key points:

## 82.2.6 Block Distribution
- 66-bit blocks are distributed to 4 PCS lanes in round-robin fashion
- Block 0 → Lane 0, Block 1 → Lane 1, Block 2 → Lane 2, Block 3 → Lane 3, Block 4 → Lane 0, etc.

## 82.2.7 Alignment Marker Insertion
- AM is inserted after every **16383** 66-bit blocks on each PCS lane (not 16384 as I thought before!)
- AM format: 66-bit block with control block sync header (10)
- AM is NOT scrambled
- AM interrupts any data transfer in progress

### 40GBASE-R AM Values (Table 82-3):
| Lane | {M0, M1, M2, BIP3, M4, M5, M6, BIP7} |
|------|---------------------------------------|
| 0 | 0x90, 0x76, 0x47, BIP3, 0x6F, 0x89, 0xB8, BIP7 |
| 1 | 0xF0, 0xC4, 0xE6, BIP3, 0x0F, 0x3B, 0x19, BIP7 |
| 2 | 0xC5, 0x65, 0x9B, BIP3, 0x3A, 0x9A, 0x64, BIP7 |
| 3 | 0xA2, 0x79, 0x3D, BIP3, 0x5D, 0x86, 0xC2, BIP7 |

Note: M4-M6 are bit-wise inversion of M0-M2, and BIP7 is bit-wise inversion of BIP3.

## 82.2.8 BIP Calculations
- BIP3 is 8 bits (bit 0-7)
- Each BIP bit is an even parity calculation over specific bit positions across all 16384 66-bit words
- BIP3 bit assignments (Table 82-4):
  - Bit 0: bits 2, 10, 18, 26, 34, 42, 50, 58 of each 66-bit word
  - Bit 1: bits 3, 11, 19, 27, 35, 43, 51, 59
  - Bit 2: bits 4, 12, 20, 28, 36, 44, 52, 60
  - Bit 3: bits 0, 5, 13, 21, 29, 37, 45, 53, 61 (includes sync header bit 0)
  - Bit 4: bits 1, 6, 14, 22, 30, 38, 46, 54, 62 (includes sync header bit 1)
  - Bit 5: bits 7, 15, 23, 31, 39, 47, 55, 63
  - Bit 6: bits 8, 16, 24, 32, 40, 48, 56, 64
  - Bit 7: bits 9, 17, 25, 33, 41, 49, 57, 65

- BIP3 and BIP7 are transmitted LSB to MSB
- BIP calculation covers bits from the previous AM to the current AM (not including the current AM)

Now I need to update the design documents with this information. The key corrections are:
1. AM is inserted after every **16383** blocks (not 16384)
2. The AM values are now confirmed
3. BIP calculation is per-lane, and the bit assignments are specific

Let me also check the existing design documents to see what needs to be updated.

现在我已经仔细阅读了 IEEE 802.3-2018 Clause 82.2 的相关章节。让我总结关键发现：

## 关键发现

### 82.2.6 Block Distribution
- 66-bit 块按 round-robin 方式分配到 4 个 PCS lane

### 82.2.7 Alignment Marker Insertion
**重要修正**：AM 在每 **16383** 个块后插入（不是 16384！）

**40GBASE-R AM 值（Table 82-3）**：
| Lane | M0 | M1 | M2 | BIP3 | M4 | M5 | M6 | BIP7 |
|------|-----|-----|-----|------|-----|-----|-----|------|
| 0 | 0x90 | 0x76 | 0x47 | BIP3 | 0x6F | 0x89 | 0xB8 | BIP7 |
| 1 | 0xF0 | 0xC4 | 0xE6 | BIP3 | 0x0F | 0x3B | 0x19 | BIP7 |
| 2 | 0xC5 | 0x65 | 0x9B | BIP3 | 0x3A | 0x9A | 0x64 | BIP7 |
| 3 | 0xA2 | 0x79 | 0x3D | BIP3 | 0x5D | 0x86 | 0xC2 | BIP7 |

特性：
- M4-M6 是 M0-M2 的按位取反
- BIP7 是 BIP3 的按位取反
- AM 不加扰

### 82.2.8 BIP Calculations
BIP3 是 8-bit 偶校验，每个 bit 的计算范围（Table 82-4）：

| BIP3 bit | 计算的 66-bit word bit 位置 |
|----------|---------------------------|
| 0 | 2, 10, 18, 26, 34, 42, 50, 58 |
| 1 | 3, 11, 19, 27, 35, 43, 51, 59 |
| 2 | 4, 12, 20, 28, 36, 44, 52, 60 |
| 3 | **0**, 5, 13, 21, 29, 37, 45, 53, 61 |
| 4 | **1**, 6, 14, 22, 30, 38, 46, 54, 62 |
| 5 | 7, 15, 23, 31, 39, 47, 55, 63 |
| 6 | 8, 16, 24, 32, 40, 48, 56, 64 |
| 7 | 9, 17, 25, 33, 41, 49, 57, 65 |

**注意**：BIP3 bit 3 和 bit 4 包含 sync header 的两个 bit！

1: # eth_pcs_am_insert 模块设计
2: 
3: ## 1. 模块概述
4: 
5: **模块名称**: eth_pcs_am_insert
6: 
7: **功能**: 块计数与对齐标记 (Alignment Marker) 插入指示
8: 
9: **位置**: rtl/pcs/eth_pcs_am_insert.sv
10: 
11: ## 2. 接口定义
12: 
13: ```systemverilog
14: module eth_pcs_am_insert (
15:     input  wire                  clk,
16:     input  wire                  rst_n,
17: 
18:     // 输入: 2个66-bit 块 (来自加扰器)
19:     input  wire [65:0]           in_block0,
20:     input  wire [65:0]           in_block1,
21:     input  wire                  in_valid,
22:     output wire                  in_ready,
23: 
24:     // 输出: 2个66-bit 块
25:     output wire [65:0]           out_block0,
26:     output wire [65:0]           out_block1,
27:     output wire                  out_valid,
28:     input  wire                  out_ready,
29: 
30:     // AM 插入指示 (输出给 eth_pcs_lane_dist)
31:     output wire                  am_insert
32: );
33: ```
34: 
35: ### 2.1 信号说明
36: 
37: **输入**:
38: - `in_block0[65:0]`: 第一个 66-bit 块
39: - `in_block1[65:0]`: 第二个 66-bit 块
40: - `in_valid`: 块有效
41: - `in_ready`: 上游就绪
42: 
43: **输出**:
44: - `out_block0[65:0]`: 第一个 66-bit 块
45: - `out_block1[65:0]`: 第二个 66-bit 块
46: - `out_valid`: 块有效
47: - `out_ready`: 下游就绪
48: - `am_insert`: AM 插入指示（高电平表示下一周期需要插入 AM）
49: 
50: ## 3. 功能描述
51: 
52: ### 3.1 设计策略
53: 
54: AM 插入分为两个模块完成：
55: 
56: 1. **eth_pcs_am_insert**: 块计数 + AM 插入指示
57: 2. **eth_pcs_lane_dist**: 根据 `am_insert` 信号插入对应 lane 的 AM，并处理反压
58: 
59: **原因**:
60: - 每个 lane 需要插入不同的 AM 值
61: - `eth_pcs_lane_dist` 模块知道当前输出到哪个 lane
62: - 反压由 `eth_pcs_lane_dist` 处理，通过 `out_ready` 信号传递
63: 
64: ### 3.2 AM 插入规则
65: 
66: 根据 IEEE 802.3ba Clause 82:
67: 
68: - **每个 lane 独立计数**: 每 16384 个块插入一次 AM
69: - **4 个 lane 同步插入**: 在同一时刻插入
70: - **插入位置**: AM 替换数据/控制块
71: 
72: ### 3.3 计数逻辑
73: 
74: **lane 分布关系**:
75: ```
76: 每周期输入: 2 个 66-bit 块
77: lane 分布: 
78:   - 周期 N:   block0 → lane0, block1 → lane1
79:   - 周期 N+1: block0 → lane2, block1 → lane3
80:   - 周期 N+2: block0 → lane0, block1 → lane1
81:   - ...
82: 
83: 每 2 个周期: 4 个 lane 各得到 1 个块
84: ```
85: 
86: **计数计算**:
87: - 每个 lane 每 16384 个块插入一次 AM
88: - 每 2 个周期，4 个 lane 各得到 1 个块
89: - 所以每 32768 个周期（或 65536 个输入块），每个 lane 得到 16384 个块
90: - 此时应该插入 AM
91: 
92: **计数器**:
93: - 16-bit 计数器
94: - 范围：0 ~ 65535
95: - 每周期 +2（处理 2 个块）
96: - 计数到 65534 时，输出 `am_insert = 1`
97: 
98: ### 3.4 AM 值定义
99: 
100: AM 值在 `eth_pcs_lane_dist` 模块中定义，每个 lane 不同。
101: 
102: ## 4. 详细设计
103: 
104: ### 4.1 块计数器
105: 
106: ```systemverilog
107: // 块计数器: 16-bit，范围 0 ~ 65535
108: // 每周期处理 2 个块，计数器每次 +2
109: reg [15:0] block_cnt;
110: 
111: always @(posedge clk) begin
112:     if (!rst_n) begin
113:         block_cnt <= 16'h0;
114:     end else if (in_valid && out_ready) begin
115:         if (block_cnt >= 16'd65534) begin
116:             block_cnt <= 16'h0;
117:         end else begin
118:             block_cnt <= block_cnt + 16'd2;
119:         end
120:     end
121: end
122: ```
123: 
124: ### 4.2 AM 插入指示
125: 
126: ```systemverilog
127: // 当 block_cnt == 65534 时，表示已处理 65534 个块
128: // 下一周期需要插入 AM，此时拉高 am_insert 信号
129: assign am_insert = (block_cnt == 16'd65534) && in_valid && out_ready;
130: ```
131: 
132: ### 4.3 数据直通
133: 
134: ```systemverilog
135: // 数据直通，无延迟
136: assign out_block0 = in_block0;
137: assign out_block1 = in_block1;
138: assign out_valid  = in_valid;
139: assign in_ready   = out_ready;
140: ```
141: 
142: ## 5. 完整实现
143: 
144: ```systemverilog
145: module eth_pcs_am_insert (
146:     input  wire                  clk,
147:     input  wire                  rst_n,
148: 
149:     // 输入: 2个66-bit 块
150:     input  wire [65:0]           in_block0,
151:     input  wire [65:0]           in_block1,
152:     input  wire                  in_valid,
153:     output wire                  in_ready,
154: 
155:     // 输出: 2个66-bit 块
156:     output wire [65:0]           out_block0,
157:     output wire [65:0]           out_block1,
158:     output wire                  out_valid,
159:     input  wire                  out_ready,
160: 
161:     // AM 插入指示
162:     output wire                  am_insert
163: );
164: 
165:     // 块计数器 (16-bit, 0 ~ 65535)
166:     reg [15:0] block_cnt;
167: 
168:     always @(posedge clk) begin
169:         if (!rst_n) begin
170:             block_cnt <= 16'h0;
171:         end else if (in_valid && out_ready) begin
172:             if (block_cnt >= 16'd65534) begin
173:                 block_cnt <= 16'h0;
174:             end else begin
175:                 block_cnt <= block_cnt + 16'd2;
176:             end
177:         end
178:     end
179: 
180:     // AM 插入指示
181:     assign am_insert = (block_cnt == 16'd65534) && in_valid && out_ready;
182: 
183:     // 数据直通
184:     assign out_block0 = in_block0;
185:     assign out_block1 = in_block1;
186:     out_valid  = in_valid;
187:     assign in_ready   = out_ready;
188: 
189: endmodule
190: ```
191: 
192: ## 6. 与 lane_dist 的配合
193: 
194: ### 6.1 反压处理
195: 
196: `eth_pcs_lane_dist` 模块接收 `am_insert=1` 后：
197: 
198: 1. 拉低 `out_ready`，反压传递到上游
199: 2. 在 2 个周期内输出 4 个 lane 的 AM
200: 3. 恢复 `out_ready`，继续正常数据分发
201: 
202: ### 6.2 时序示例
203: 
204: ```
205: 周期:        |  N    | N+1   | N+2   | N+3   | N+4   |
206:              |       |       |       |       |       |
207: block_cnt:   | 65532 | 65534 |   0   |   2   |   4   |
208:              |       |       |       |       |       |
209: am_insert:   |   0   |   1   |   0   |   0   |   0   |
210:              |       |       |       |       |       |
211: out_ready:   |   1   |   1   |   0   |   0   |   1   |  ← lane_dist 反压
212:              |       |       |       |       |       |
213: in_block0:   | D0    | D2    | D2    | D2    | D4    |
214: in_block1:   | D1    | D3    | D3    | D3    | D5    |
215:              |       |       |       |       |       |
216: lane_dist:   |       |       |       |       |       |
217:   output:    | D0→L0 | D2→L0 | AM_L0 | AM_L2 | D4→L0 |
218:              | D1→L1 | D3→L1 | AM_L1 | AM_L3 | D5→L1 |
219: ```
220: 
221: ## 7. 流水线
222: 
223: 本模块为直通模式，无流水线延迟：
224: 
225: ```
226: clk:         |   N   |  N+1  |
227:              |       |       |
228: in_block0    |  B0   |  B1   |
229: in_block1    |  B1   |  B2   |
230: in_valid     |___/   |   \___|
231:              |       |       |
232: out_block0   |  B0   |  B1   |
233: out_block1   |  B1   |  B2   |
234: out_valid    |___/   |   \___|
235: ```
236: 
237: ## 8. 数据流位置
238: 
239: ```
240: TX: eth_pcs_64b66b_enc → eth_pcs_scrambler → eth_pcs_am_insert → eth_pcs_lane_dist
241: ```
242: 
243: ## 9. 参考文献
244: 
245: - IEEE 802.3-2018 Clause 82.2.6 (Alignment Marker)
246: - IEEE 802.3-2018 Clause 83.2.6 (AM Insertion)
247: 
248: ## 10. 修订历史
249: 
250: | 版本 | 日期 | 描述 |
251: |------|------|------|
252: | 1.0 | 2026-04-10 | 初始版本 |
253: | 1.1 | 2026-04-10 | 修正计数器为16-bit，计数范围0~65535 |

(End of file - total 253 lines)
</content>
```

<content>
1: # eth_pcs_lane_dist 模块设计
2: 
3: ## 1. 模块概述
4: 
5: **模块名称**: eth_pcs_lane_dist
6: 
7: **功能**: Lane 分布，将 66-bit 块流分发到 4 个 lane，并处理 AM 插入
8: 
9: **位置**: rtl/pcs/eth_pcs_lane_dist.sv
10: 
11: ## 2. 接口定义
12: 
13: ```systemverilog
14: module eth_pcs_lane_dist (
15:     input  wire                  clk,
16:     input  wire                  rst_n,
17: 
18:     // 输入: 2个66-bit 块 (来自 am_insert)
19:     input  wire [65:0]           in_block0,
20:     input  wire [65:0]           in_block1,
21:     input  wire                  in_valid,
22:     output wire                  in_ready,
23: 
24:     // AM 插入指示
25:     input  wire                  am_insert,
26: 
27:     // 输出: 4个lane的66-bit 块 (每周期输出2个lane)
28:     output wire [65:0]           lane0_block,
29:     output wire [65:0]           lane1_block,
30:     output wire                  lane_valid,
31:     input  wire                  lane_ready
32: );
33: ```
34: 
35: ### 2.1 信号说明
36: 
37: **输入**:
38: - `in_block0[65:0]`: 第一个 66-bit 块
39: - `in_block1[65:0]`: 第二个 66-bit 块
40: - `in_valid`: 块有效
41: - `in_ready`: 上游就绪
42: - `am_insert`: AM 插入指示（高电平表示需要插入 AM）
43: 
44: **输出**:
45: - `lane0_block[65:0]`: Lane 0 的 66-bit 块
46: - `lane1_block[65:0]`: Lane 1 的 66-bit 块
47: - `lane_valid`: 块有效
48: - `lane_ready`: 下游就绪
49: 
50: > 注：每周期输出 2 个 lane 的数据，Lane 2 和 Lane 3 在下一周期输出。
51: 
52: ## 3. 功能描述
53: 
54: ### 3.1 Lane 分布规则
55: 
56: 每周期输入 2 个 66-bit 块，分发到 4 个 lane：
57: 
58: ```
59: 周期 N:   block0 → Lane 0,  block1 → Lane 1
60: 周期 N+1: block0 → Lane 2,  block1 → Lane 3
61: 周期 N+2: block0 → Lane 0,  block1 → Lane 1
62: ...
63: ```
64: 
65: ### 3.2 输出格式
66: 
67: 每周期输出 2 个 lane 的数据：
68: 
69: ```
70: 周期 N:   输出 Lane 0 和 Lane 1
71: 周期 N+1: 输出 Lane 2 和 Lane 3
72: 周期 N+2: 输出 Lane 0 和 Lane 1
73: ...
74: ```
75: 
76: ### 3.3 AM 插入
77: 
78: 当 `am_insert = 1` 时：
79: 
80: 1. 暂停接收上游数据（拉低 `in_ready`）
81: 2. 在 2 个周期内输出 4 个 lane 的 AM
82: 3. 恢复正常数据分发
83: 
84: ## 4. 详细设计
85: 
86: ### 4.1 Lane 选择计数器
87: 
88: ```systemverilog
89: // Lane 选择计数器: 1-bit
90: // 0: 输出 Lane 0/1
91: // 1: 输出 Lane 2/3
92: reg lane_sel;
93: 
94: always @(posedge clk) begin
95:     if (!rst_n) begin
96:         lane_sel <= 1'b0;
97:     end else if (lane_valid && lane_ready) begin
98:         lane_sel <= ~lane_sel;
99:     end
100: end
101: ```
102: 
103: ### 4.2 AM 插入状态机
104: 
105: ```systemverilog
106: // 状态定义
107: typedef enum logic [1:0] {
108:     NORMAL,      // 正常数据分发
109:     AM_INSERT_0, // AM 插入周期 0 (Lane 0, 1)
110:     AM_INSERT_1  // AM 插入周期 1 (Lane 2, 3)
111: } state_t;
112: 
113: reg [1:0] state;
114: 
115: always @(posedge clk) begin
116:     if (!rst_n) begin
117:         state <= NORMAL;
118:     end else begin
119:         case (state)
120:             NORMAL: begin
121:                 if (am_insert && in_valid && lane_ready) begin
122:                     state <= AM_INSERT_0;
123:                 end
124:             end
125:             AM_INSERT_0: begin
126:                 if (lane_ready) begin
127:                     state <= AM_INSERT_1;
128:                 end
129:             end
130:             AM_INSERT_1: begin
131:                 if (lane_ready) begin
132:                     state <= NORMAL;
133:                 end
134:             end
135:             default: state <= NORMAL;
136:         endcase
137:     end
138: end
139: ```
140: 
141: ### 4.3 AM 值定义
142: 
143: ```systemverilog
144: // AM 值定义 (根据 IEEE 802.3ba Clause 82.2.6)
145: // 注: 实际值需查阅标准确认
146: localparam [65:0] AM_LANE0 = 66'h2B_xxxx_xxxx_xxxx_xxxx;  // 待确认
147: localparam [65:0] AM_LANE1 = 66'h2B_xxxx_xxxx_xxxx_xxxx;  // 待确认
148: localparam [65:0] AM_LANE2 = 66'h2B_xxxx_xxxx_xxxx_xxxx;  // 待确认
149: localparam [65:0] AM_LANE3 = 66'h2B_xxxx_xxxx_xxxx_xxxx;  // 待确认
150: ```
151: 
152: ### 4.4 输出逻辑
153: 
154: ```systemverilog
155: // 输出数据选择
156: reg [65:0] lane0_block_reg;
157: reg [65:0] lane1_block_reg;
158: 
159: always @(*) begin
160:     case (state)
161:         NORMAL: begin
162:             if (lane_sel == 1'b0) begin
163:                 // 输出 Lane 0, 1
164:                 lane0_block_reg = in_block0;
165:                 lane1_block_reg = in_block1;
166:             end else begin
167:                 // 输出 Lane 2, 3
168:                 lane0_block_reg = in_block0;
169:                 lane1_block_reg = in_block1;
170:             end
171:         end
172:         AM_INSERT_0: begin
173:             // 输出 Lane 0, 1 的 AM
174:             lane0_block_reg = AM_LANE0;
175:             lane1_block_reg = AM_LANE1;
176:         end
177:         AM_INSERT_1: begin
178:             // 输出 Lane 2, 3 的 AM
179:             lane0_block_reg = AM_LANE2;
180:             lane1_block_reg = AM_LANE3;
181:         end
182:         default: begin
183:             lane0_block_reg = 66'h0;
184:             lane1_block_reg = 66'h0;
185:         end
186:     endcase
187: end
188: 
189: assign lane0_block = lane0_block_reg;
190: assign lane1_block = lane1_block_reg;
191: ```
192: 
193: ### 4.5 握手信号
194: 
195: ```systemverilog
196: // lane_valid: 输出有效
197: // 正常模式或 AM 插入模式都输出有效数据
198: assign lane_valid = in_valid || (state != NORMAL);
199: 
200: // in_ready: 上游就绪
201: // 正常模式: 跟随 lane_ready
202: // AM 插入模式: 拉低，暂停上游
203: assign in_ready = (state == NORMAL) ? lane_ready : 1'b0;
204: ```
205: 
206: ## 5. 完整实现
207: 
208: ```systemverilog
209: module eth_pcs_lane_dist (
210:     input  wire                  clk,
211:     input  wire                  rst_n,
212: 
213:     // 输入: 2个66-bit 块
214:     input  wire [65:0]           in_block0,
215:     input  wire [65:0]           in_block1,
216:     input  wire                  in_valid,
217:     output wire                  in_ready,
218: 
219:     // AM 插入指示
220:     input  wire                  am_insert,
221: 
222:     // 输出: 2个lane的66-bit 块
223:     output wire [65:0]           lane0_block,
224:     output wire [65:0]           lane1_block,
225:     output wire                  lane_valid,
226:     input  wire                  lane_ready
227: );
228: 
229:     // 状态定义
230:     typedef enum logic [1:0] {
231:         NORMAL,      // 正常数据分发
232:         AM_INSERT_0, // AM 插入周期 0 (Lane 0, 1)
233:         AM_INSERT_1  // AM 插入周期 1 (Lane 2, 3)
234:     } state_t;
235: 
236:     reg [1:0] state;
237:     reg       lane_sel;
238: 
239:     // AM 值定义 (待确认)
240:     localparam [65:0] AM_LANE0 = 66'h2B_00000000_00000000;  // 待确认
241:     localparam [65:0] AM_LANE1 = 66'h2B_00000000_00000001;  // 待确认
242:     localparam [65:0] AM_LANE2 = 66'h2B_00000000_00000002;  // 待确认
243:     localparam [65:0] AM_LANE3 = 66'h2B_00000000_00000003;  // 待确认
244: 
245:     // 状态机
246:     always @(posedge clk) begin
247:         if (!rst_n) begin
248:             state <= NORMAL;
249:         end else begin
250:             case (state)
251:                 NORMAL: begin
252:                     if (am_insert && in_valid && lane_ready) begin
253:                         state <= AM_INSERT_0;
254:                     end
255:                 end
256:                 AM_INSERT_0: begin
257:                     if (lane_ready) begin
258:                         state <= AM_INSERT_1;
259:                     end
260:                 end
261:                 AM_INSERT_1: begin
262:                     if (lane_ready) begin
263:                         state <= NORMAL;
264:                     end
265:                 end
266:                 default: state <= NORMAL;
267:             endcase
268:         end
269:     end
270: 
271:     // Lane 选择计数器
272:     always @(posedge clk) begin
273:         if (!rst_n) begin
274:             lane_sel <= 1'b0;
275:         end else if (state == NORMAL && lane_valid && lane_ready) begin
276:             lane_sel <= ~lane_sel;
277:         end
278:     end
279: 
280:     // 输出数据选择
281:     reg [65:0] lane0_block_reg;
282:     reg [65:0] lane1_block_reg;
283: 
284:     always @(*) begin
285:         case (state)
286:             NORMAL: begin
287:                 lane0_block_reg = in_block0;
288:                 lane1_block_reg = in_block1;
289:             end
290:             AM_INSERT_0: begin
291:                 lane0_block_reg = AM_LANE0;
292:                 lane1_block_reg = AM_LANE1;
293:             end
294:             AM_INSERT_1: begin
295:                 lane0_block_reg = AM_LANE2;
296:                 lane1_block_reg = AM_LANE3;
297:             end
298:             default: begin
299:                 lane0_block_reg = 66'h0;
300:                 lane1_block_reg = 66'h0;
301:             end
302:         endcase
303:     end
304: 
305:     assign lane0_block = lane0_block_reg;
306:     assign lane1_block = lane1_block_reg;
307: 
308:     // 握手信号
309:     assign lane_valid = (state == NORMAL) ? in_valid : 1'b1;
310:     assign in_ready   = (state == NORMAL) ? lane_ready : 1'b0;
311: 
312: endmodule
313: ```
314: 
315: ## 6. 时序图
316: 
317: ### 6.1 正常数据分发
318: 
319: ```
320: 周期:        |   N   |  N+1  |  N+2  |  N+3  |
321:              |       |       |       |       |
322: lane_sel:    |   0   |   1   |   0   |   1   |
323:              |       |       |       |       |
324: in_block0:   |  D0   |  D2   |  D4   |  D6   |
325: in_block1:   |  D1   |  D3   |  D5   |  D7   |
326:              |       |       |       |       |
327: lane0_block: |  D0   |  D2   |  D4   |  D6   | → Lane 0/2
328: lane1_block: |  D1   |  D3   |  D5   |  D7   | → Lane 1/3
329:              |       |       |       |       |
330: 输出:        | L0,L1 | L2,L3 | L0,L1 | L2,L3 |
331: ```
332: 
333: ### 6.2 AM 插入
334: 
335: ```
336: 周期:        |   N   |  N+1  |  N+2  |  N+3  |  N+4  |
337:              |       |       |       |       |       |
338: am_insert:   |   0   |   1   |   0   |   0   |   0   |
339:              |       |       |       |       |       |
340: state:       |NORMAL |NORMAL |AM_INS0|AM_INS1|NORMAL |
341:              |       |       |       |       |       |
342: in_ready:    |   1   |   1   |   0   |   0   |   1   |
343:              |       |       |       |       |       |
344: in_block0:   |  D0   |  D2   |  D2   |  D2   |  D4   |
345: in_block1:   |  D1   |  D3   |  D3   |  D3   |  D5   |
346:              |       |       |       |       |       |

348: lane1_block: |  D1   |  D3   | AM_L1 | AM_L3 |  D5   |
349:              |       |       |       |       |       |
350: 输出:        | L0,L1 | L2,L3 | L0,L1 | L2,L3 | L0,L1 |
351: ```
352: 
353: ## 7. 数据流位置
354: 
355: ```
356: TX: eth_pcs_am_insert → eth_pcs_lane_dist → eth_pcs_gearbox_tx
357: ```

368: | 1.0 | 2026-04-10 | 初始版本 |

_Thinking:_

现在我发现了几个需要修正的问题：

1. **AM 插入周期错误**：文档中写的是 16384 个块，但标准说的是 **16383** 个块后插入 AM

2. **AM 值缺失**：现在可以从 Table 82-3 获取正确的 AM 值

3. **BIP 计算缺失**：需要实现 BIP-3 的计算逻辑

让我整理一下需要讨论和修正的内容：

### AM 插入周期
标准说 "The alignment markers shall be inserted after every 16383 66-bit blocks on each PCS lane."
这意味着：
- 每个 lane 在 16383 个块后插入 AM
- 16383 个块 = 16384 个块周期（从上一个 AM 后开始计数）

### AM 值（40GBASE-R）
根据 Table 82-3：
- Lane 0: 0x90, 0x76, 0x47, BIP3, 0x6F, 0x89, 0xB8, BIP7
- Lane 1: 0xF0, 0xC4, 0xE6, BIP3, 0x0F, 0x3B, 0x19, BIP7
- Lane 2: 0xC5, 0x65, 0x9B, BIP3, 0x3A, 0x9A, 0x64, BIP7
- Lane 3: 0xA2, 0x79, 0x3D, BIP3, 0x5D, 0x86, 0xC2, BIP7

AM 格式（Figure 82-9）：
- Bit 0-1: Sync header (10)
- Bit 2-9: M0
- Bit 10-17: M1
- Bit 18-25: M2
- Bit 26-33: BIP3
- Bit 34-41: M4
- Bit 42-49: M5
- Bit 50-57: M6
- Bit 58-65: BIP7

### BIP 计算
BIP3 是 8-bit 偶校验，计算范围：
- 从上一个 AM（不包括）到当前 AM（不包括）之间的所有块
- 每个 bit 计算特定位置的 XOR

BIP3 bit 分配（Table 82-4）：
- BIP3[0]: bits 2, 10, 18, 26, 34, 42, 50, 58
- BIP3[1]: bits 3, 11, 19, 27, 35, 43, 51, 59
- BIP3[2]: bits 4, 12, 20, 28, 36, 44, 52, 60
- BIP3[3]: bits 0, 5, 13, 21, 29, 37, 45, 53, 61 (包含 sync header bit 0)
- BIP3[4]: bits 1, 6, 14, 22, 30, 38, 46, 54, 62 (包含 sync header bit 1)
- BIP3[5]: bits 7, 15, 23, 31, 39, 47, 55, 63
- BIP3[6]: bits 8, 16, 24, 32, 40, 48, 56, 64
- BIP3[7]: bits 9, 17, 25, 33, 41, 49, 57, 65

现在需要讨论：
1. BIP 计算应该在哪里实现？
2. 如何传递 BIP 值？
3. AM 插入周期的修正

根据 IEEE 802.3-2018 标准，我发现以下需要修正的问题：

## 发现的问题

### 1. AM 插入周期错误
**标准原文**: "The alignment markers shall be inserted after every **16383** 66-bit blocks on each PCS lane."

当前文档写的是 16384，应该是 **16383**。

### 2. AM 值已确认（40GBASE-R Table 82-3）

| Lane | M0 | M1 | M2 | BIP3 | M4 | M5 | M6 | BIP7 |
|------|------|------|------|------|------|------|------|------|
| 0 | 0x90 | 0x76 | 0x47 | 动态 | 0x6F | 0x89 | 0xB8 | ~BIP3 |
| 1 | 0xF0 | 0xC4 | 0xE6 | 动态 | 0x0F | 0x3B | 0x19 | ~BIP3 |
| 2 | 0xC5 | 0x65 | 0x9B | 动态 | 0x3A | 0x9A | 0x64 | ~BIP3 |
| 3 | 0xA2 | 0x79 | 0x3D | 动态 | 0x5D | 0x86 | 0xC2 | ~BIP3 |

**AM 格式** (66-bit，LSB first):
```
Bit 0-1:   Sync Header = 10 (control block)
Bit 2-9:   M0
Bit 10-17: M1
Bit 18-25: M2
Bit 26-33: BIP3
Bit 34-41: M4 (= ~M0)
Bit 42-49: M5 (= ~M1)
Bit 50-57: M6 (= ~M2)
Bit 58-65: BIP7 (= ~BIP3)
```

### 3. BIP 计算规则（Table 82-4）

BIP3 是 8-bit 偶校验，每个 bit 对应 66-bit 块中的特定位置：

| BIP3 bit | 计算的 bit 位置 |
|----------|----------------|
| 0 | 2, 10, 18, 26, 34, 42, 50, 58 |
| 1 | 3, 11, 19, 27, 35, 43, 51, 59 |
| 2 | 4, 12, 20, 28, 36, 44, 52, 60 |
| 3 | **0**, 5, 13, 21, 29, 37, 45, 53, 61 |
| 4 | **1**, 6, 14, 22, 30, 38, 46, 54, 62 |
| 5 | 7, 15, 23, 31, 39, 47, 55, 63 |
| 6 | 8, 16, 24, 32, 40, 48, 56, 64 |
| 7 | 9, 17, 25, 33, 41, 49, 57, 65 |

**注意**: BIP3[3] 和 BIP3[4] 包含 sync header 的两个 bit！

---

## 需要讨论的设计决策

### BIP 计算应该在哪里实现？

**方案 A**: 在 `eth_pcs_am_insert` 中计算
- 优点：集中处理 AM 相关逻辑
- 缺点：需要为每个 lane 独立计算 BIP

**方案 B**: 在 `eth_pcs_lane_dist` 中计算
- 优点：数据分发后，每个 lane 独立计算更自然
- 缺点：需要缓存输入数据

**方案 C**: 在 `eth_pcs_am_insert` 中计算，但只计算一个 BIP 值
- 由于 BIP 是对每个 lane 独立计算的，而数据是 round-robin 分发的，需要在分发后分别计算

我建议采用 **方案 B**：在 `eth_pcs_lane_dist` 中计算每个 lane 的 BIP，因为：
1. 每个 lane 需要独立的 BIP 累加器
2. 数据分发后，每个 lane 的数据流是独立的
3. 逻辑更清晰

你希望如何处理？

---

## User

按方案B实现

---

## Assistant (Build · Astron Coding Plan · 141.4s)

_Thinking:_

用户确认按方案B实现，即在 `eth_pcs_lane_dist` 中计算每个 lane 的 BIP。

我需要更新两个设计文档：
1. `eth_pcs_am_insert.md` - 修正 AM 插入周期（16383 而不是 16384），移除 BIP 相关内容（因为 BIP 在 lane_dist 中计算）
2. `eth_pcs_lane_dist.md` - 添加 BIP 计算逻辑，添加正确的 AM 值

让我先仔细理解 BIP 计算逻辑：

BIP3 是 8-bit 偶校验值，每个 bit 对应 66-bit 块中的特定位置：
- BIP3[0] = XOR of bits 2, 10, 18, 26, 34, 42, 50, 58 (每块8个bit)
- BIP3[1] = XOR of bits 3, 11, 19, 27, 35, 43, 51, 59 (每块8个bit)
- BIP3[2] = XOR of bits 4, 12, 20, 28, 36, 44, 52, 60 (每块8个bit)
- BIP3[3] = XOR of bits 0, 5, 13, 21, 29, 37, 45, 53, 61 (每块9个bit，包含sync header bit 0)
- BIP3[4] = XOR of bits 1, 6, 14, 22, 30, 38, 46, 54, 62 (每块9个bit，包含sync header bit 1)
- BIP3[5] = XOR of bits 7, 15, 23, 31, 39, 47, 55, 63 (每块8个bit)
- BIP3[6] = XOR of bits 8, 16, 24, 32, 40, 48, 56, 64 (每块8个bit)
- BIP3[7] = XOR of bits 9, 17, 25, 33, 41, 49, 57, 65 (每块8个bit)

BIP 计算范围：从上一个 AM 到当前 AM 之间的所有数据块（不包括 AM 本身）。

每个 lane 独立计算 BIP。

现在让我更新设计文档。

首先，关于 AM 插入周期的修正：
- 标准说 "after every 16383 66-bit blocks on each PCS lane"
- 这意味着每个 lane 在 16383 个数据块后插入一个 AM
- 所以每个 lane 的周期是 16384 个块（16383 数据块 + 1 AM）

对于整个系统：
- 4 个 lane 同步插入 AM
- 每 16384 个块（每个 lane），插入一次 AM
- 由于 round-robin 分发，每 16384*4 = 65536 个输入块，插入一次 AM

等等，让我重新理解：
- 每个 lane 独立计数，每 16383 个数据块后插入 AM
- AM 插入是同步的，所有 lane 同时插入
- 所以当 lane 0 计数到 16383 时，lane 1、2、3 也应该计数到 16383

由于 round-robin 分发：
- 输入块 0 → lane 0
- 输入块 1 → lane 1
- 输入块 2 → lane 2
- 输入块 3 → lane 3
- 输入块 4 → lane 0
- ...

所以当 lane 0 收到第 16383 个块时，lane 1 收到第 16383 个块（输入块 16383*4+1），等等。

这意味着每 16384*4 = 65536 个输入块，所有 lane 同时插入 AM。

但标准说的是 "after every 16383 66-bit blocks"，这意味着：
- lane 0: 块 0, 1, 2, ..., 16382 (共 16383 个)，然后插入 AM
- 所以是每 16384 个块周期（16383 数据 + 1 AM）

让我重新计算：
- 每个 lane 每 16384 个块（包括 AM）为一个周期
- 其中 16383 个是数据块，1 个是 AM
- 4 个 lane 同步，所以每 16384*4 = 65536 个输入块周期

但当前设计是每周期处理 2 个块，所以：
- 每 65536/2 = 32768 个周期，插入一次 AM

计数器范围：
- 如果从 0 开始，每周期 +2
- 计数到 65534 时，下一周期插入 AM
- 所以计数器范围是 0 到 65534（共 32768 个周期）

等等，让我重新理解标准：
"The alignment markers shall be inserted after every 16383 66-bit blocks on each PCS lane."

这意味着：
- 每个 lane 收到 16383 个数据块后，插入一个 AM
- 然后继续接收数据块

所以：
- Lane 0: 数据块 0-16382 (16383个) → AM → 数据块 16383-32765 (16383个) → AM → ...
- Lane 1: 同样
- ...

由于 round-robin：
- 输入块 0 → lane 0
- 输入块 1 → lane 1
- 输入块 2 → lane 2
- 输入块 3 → lane 3
- 输入块 4 → lane 0
- ...
- 输入块 65532 → lane 0 (lane 0 的第 16383 个块)
- 输入块 65533 → lane 1 (lane 1 的第 16383 个块)
- 输入块 65534 → lane 2 (lane 2 的第 16383 个块)
- 输入块 65535 → lane 3 (lane 3 的第 16383 个块)
- 然后插入 AM

所以：
- 每 65536 个输入块，插入一次 AM
- 当前设计每周期处理 2 个块，所以每 32768 个周期插入一次 AM

计数器：
- 16-bit 计数器，范围 0 到 65535
- 每周期 +2
- 当计数器 = 65534 时，表示已处理 65534 个块
- 当计数器 = 65534 且 in_valid && out_ready 时，下一个周期插入 AM

实际上，当前设计文档的计数逻辑是正确的：
- 计数器从 0 开始，每周期 +2
- 当计数器 = 65534 时，am_insert = 1
- 这意味着已处理 65534 个块，下一周期插入 AM

但文档中写的是 "每 16384 个块插入一次 AM"，应该改为 "每 16383 个数据块后插入 AM"。

让我更新文档。

AM 值的计算：
根据 Table 82-3，40GBASE-R 的 AM 值：
- Lane 0: {M0, M1, M2, BIP3, M4, M5, M6, BIP7} = {0x90, 0x76, 0x47, BIP3, 0x6F, 0x89, 0xB8, BIP7}
- Lane 1: {0xF0, 0xC4, 0xE6, BIP3, 0x0F, 0x3B, 0x19, BIP7}
- Lane 2: {0xC5, 0x65, 0x9B, BIP3, 0x3A, 0x9A, 0x64, BIP7}
- Lane 3: {0xA2, 0x79, 0x3D, BIP3, 0x5D, 0x86, 0xC2, BIP7}

AM 格式（66-bit）：
- Bit 0-1: Sync Header = 10 (control block)
- Bit 2-9: M0 (8 bits)
- Bit 10-17: M1 (8 bits)
- Bit 18-25: M2 (8 bits)
- Bit 26-33: BIP3 (8 bits)
- Bit 34-41: M4 (8 bits)
- Bit 42-49: M5 (8 bits)
- Bit 50-57: M6 (8 bits)
- Bit 58-65: BIP7 (8 bits)

注意：标准说 "Each octet is transmitted LSB to MSB"，所以每个字节是 LSB first。

让我计算 AM 的 66-bit 值：

对于 Lane 0（假设 BIP3 = 0x00）：
- Sync Header: 10 (bit 0-1)
- M0 = 0x90: bit 2-9
- M1 = 0x76: bit 10-17
- M2 = 0x47: bit 18-25
- BIP3 = 0x00: bit 26-33
- M4 = 0x6F: bit 34-41
- M5 = 0x89: bit 42-49
- M6 = 0xB8: bit 50-57
- BIP7 = 0xFF: bit 58-65

66-bit 值（从 bit 0 到 bit 65）：
= {BIP7, M6, M5, M4, BIP3, M2, M1, M0, Sync}
= {0xFF, 0xB8, 0x89, 0x6F, 0x00, 0x47, 0x76, 0x90, 2'b10}

等等，我需要确认 bit 顺序。标准说：
"Bit Position: 0 1 2 ... 65"
"Each octet is transmitted LSB to MSB"

所以 bit 0 是最先传输的。

AM 格式：
- Bit 0-1: Sync Header = 10
- Bit 2-9: M0 (bit 2 是 M0[0], bit 9 是 M0[7])
- Bit 10-17: M1
- ...

所以 66-bit 值：
bit[1:0] = 2'b10 (sync header)
bit[9:2] = M0
bit[17:10] = M1
bit[25:18] = M2
bit[33:26] = BIP3
bit[41:34] = M4
bit[49:42] = M5
bit[57:50] = M6
bit[65:58] = BIP7

对于 Lane 0（BIP3 = 0x00, BIP7 = 0xFF）：
66-bit 值 = {8'hFF, 8'hB8, 8'h89, 8'h6F, 8'h00, 8'h47, 8'h76, 8'h90, 2'b10}

让我用 SystemVerilog 表示：
localparam [65:0] AM_LANE0_BASE = {8'hFF, 8'hB8, 8'h89, 8'h6F, 8'h00, 8'h47, 8'h76, 8'h90, 2'b10};

等等，我需要重新检查。标准中的例子：
"the lane marker for 100GBASE-R lane number 0 is sent as (left most bit sent first):
10 10000011 00010110 10000100 BIP3 01111100 11101001 01111011 BIP7"

这里 10 是 sync header，10000011 是 M0=0xC1...

让我解析：
- Sync: 10
- M0: 10000011 = 0xC1 (bit 2-9)
- M1: 00010110 = 0x16... 等等，这不对

让我重新看：
"10 10000011 00010110 10000100 BIP3 01111100 11101001 01111011 BIP7"

这是按传输顺序（bit 0 先传）：
- Bit 0-1: 10 (sync header)
- Bit 2-9: 10000011 (M0)
- Bit 10-17: 00010110 (M1)
- ...

10000011 (binary) = 0x83... 但 Table 82-2 说 Lane 0 的 M0 = 0xC1

让我检查：0xC1 = 11000001 (binary)

如果 LSB first 传输：
- 传输顺序: 10000011
- 值: bit 0 先传，所以 10000011 表示 M0[0]=1, M0[1]=1, M0[2]=0, ..., M0[7]=1
- 即 M0 = 11000001 = 0xC1

好的，我理解了。每个字节是 LSB first，所以：
- 传输序列 "10000011" 对应值 0xC1
- 传输序列 "00010110" 对应值 0x68 (Table 82-2: M1 = 0x68)

让我验证：
0x68 = 01101000 (binary)
LSB first: 00010110 ✓

好的，现在我理解了。

对于 40GBASE-R Lane 0：
- M0 = 0x90 = 10010000 (binary) → LSB first: 00001001
- M1 = 0x76 = 01110110 (binary) → LSB first: 01101110
- M2 = 0x47 = 01000111 (binary) → LSB first: 11100010
- M4 = 0x6F = 01101111 (binary) → LSB first: 11110110
- M5 = 0x89 = 10001001 (binary) → LSB first: 10010001
- M6 = 0xB8 = 10111000 (binary) → LSB first: 00011101

AM Lane 0 传输序列（假设 BIP3 = 0x00）：
10 00001001 01101110 11100010 00000000 11110110 10010001 00011101 11111111

让我计算 66-bit 值：
bit[1:0] = 2'b10
bit[9:2] = 0x90 (M0)
bit[17:10] = 0x76 (M1)
bit[25:18] = 0x47 (M2)
bit[33:26] = BIP3
bit[41:34] = 0x6F (M4)
bit[49:42] = 0x89 (M5)
bit[57:50] = 0xB8 (M6)

所以 66-bit 值（假设 BIP3 = 0x00）：

= 66'h2B_B8_89_6F_00_47_76_90

66-bit 值 = {bit[65:58], bit[57:50], bit[49:42], bit[41:34], bit[33:26], bit[25:18], bit[17:10], bit[9:2], bit[1:0]}
= {BIP7, M6, M5, M4, BIP3, M2, M1, M0, Sync}

对于 Lane 0（BIP3 = 0x00, BIP7 = 0xFF）：
= {8'hFF, 8'hB8, 8'h89, 8'h6F, 8'h00, 8'h47, 8'h76, 8'h90, 2'b10}

val = (0xFF << 58) | (0xB8 << 50) | (0x89 << 42) | (0x6F << 34) | (0x00 << 26) | (0x47 << 18) | (0x76 << 10) | (0x90 << 2) | 0b10
print(hex(val))
```

= 0xFF_B8_89_6F_00_47_76_90_2 (需要 66 bits)

让我重新组织：
bit[65:58] = BIP7 = 0xFF
bit[57:50] = M6 = 0xB8

让我用更清晰的方式：
= {2'b10, 8'h90, 8'h76, 8'h47, 8'h00, 8'h6F, 8'h89, 8'hB8, 8'hFF}

在 SystemVerilog 中：

等等，这个顺序不对。让我重新理解 SystemVerilog 的位拼接：

{A, B, C} 其中 A 是最高位，C 是最低位。

所以 {2'b10, 8'h90, ...} 表示：
- bit[65:64] = 2'b10
- bit[63:56] = 8'h90
- ...

- bit[1:0] = sync header
- bit[9:2] = M0
- ...

所以应该是：

这样：
- bit[65:58] = 8'hFF (BIP7)
- bit[57:50] = 8'hB8 (M6)
- ...
- bit[9:2] = 8'h90 (M0)
- bit[1:0] = 2'b10 (Sync)

接口定义\n\n```systemverilog\nmodule eth_pcs_am_insert (\n    input  wire                  clk,\n    input  wire                  rst_n,\n\n    input  wire [65:0]           in_block0,\n    input  wire out_block1,\n    output wire                  out_valid,\n    input  wire                  out_ready,\n\n    output wire                  am_insert\n);\n```\n\n### 2.1 信号说明\n\n**输入**:\n- `in_block0[65:0]`: 第一个 66-bit 块\n- `in_block1[65:0]`: 第二个 66-bit 块\n- `in_valid`: 块有效\n- `in_ready`: 上游就绪\n\n**输出**:\n- `out_block0[65:0]`: 第一个 66-bit 块\n- `out_block1[65:0]`: 第二个 66-bit 块\n- `out_valid`: 块有效\n- `out_ready`: 下游就绪\n- `am_insert`: AM 插入指示（高电平表示下一周期需要插入 AM）\n\n## 3. 功能描述\n\n### 3.1 设计策略\n\nAM 插入分为两个模块完成：\n\n1. **eth_pcs_am_insert**: 块计数 + AM 插入指示\n2. **eth_pcs_lane_dist**: 根据 `am_insert` 信号插入对应 lane 的 AM，计算 BIP，处理反压\n\n**原因**:\n- 每个 lane 需要插入不同的 AM 值\n- 每个 lane 需要独立计算 BIP\n- `eth_pcs_lane_dist` 模块知道当前输出到哪个 lane\n- 反压由 `eth_pcs_lane_dist` 处理，通过 `out_ready` 信号传递\n\n### 3.2 AM 插入规则\n\n根据 IEEE 802.3-2018 Clause 82.2.7:\n\n- **每个 lane 独立计数**: 每 **16383** 个数据块后插入一次 AM\n- **4 个 lane 同步插入**: 在同一时刻插入\n- **插入位置**: AM 替换数据/控制块，必要时删除 IPG\n\n### 3.3 计数逻辑\n\n**lane 分布关系**:\n```\n每周期输入: 2 个 66-bit 块\nlane 分布: \n  - 周期 N:   block0 → lane0, block1 → lane1\n  - 周期 N+1: block0 → lane2, block1 → lane3\n  - 周期 N+2: block0 → lane0, block1 → lane1\n  - ...\n\n每 2 个周期: 4 个 lane 各得到 1 个块\n```\n\n**计数计算**:\n- 每个 lane 每 16383 个数据块后插入一次 AM\n- 每 2 个周期，4 个 lane 各得到 1 个块\n- 所以每 16383 × 4 = 65532 个输入块后，每个 lane 都收到了 16383 个块\n- 此时应该插入 AM\n\n**计数器**:\n- 16-bit 计数器\n- 范围：0 ~ 65531\n- 每周期 +2（处理 2 个块）\n- 计数到 65530 时，下一周期插入 AM（`am_insert = 1`）\n\n## 4. 详细设计\n\n### 4.1 块计数器\n\n```systemverilog\nreg [15:0] block_cnt;\n\nalways @(posedge clk) begin\n    if (!rst_n) begin\n        block_cnt <= 16'h0;\n    end else if (in_valid && out_ready) begin\n        if (block_cnt >= 16'd65530) begin\n            block_cnt <= 16'h0;\n        end else begin\n            block_cnt <= block_cnt + 16'd2;\n        end\n    end\nend\n```\n\n### 4.2 AM 插入指示\n\n```systemverilog\nassign am_insert = (block_cnt == 16'd65530) && in_valid && out_ready;\n```\n\n### 4.3 数据直通\n\n```systemverilog\nassign out_block0 = in_block0;\nassign out_block1 = in_block1;\nassign out_valid  = in_valid;\nassign in_ready   = out_ready;\n```\n\n## 5. 完整实现\n\n```systemverilog\nmodule eth_pcs_am_insert (\n    input  wire                  clk,\n    input  wire                  rst_n,\n\n    input  wire [65:0]           in_block0,\n    input  wire [65:0]           in_block1,\n    input  wire                  in_valid,\n    output wire                  in_ready,\n\n    output wire [65:0]           out_block0,\n    output wire [65:0]           out_block1,\n    output wire                  out_valid,\n    input  wire                  out_ready,\n\n    output wire                  am_insert\n);\n\n    reg [15:0] block_cnt;\n\n    always @(posedge clk) begin\n        if (!rst_n) begin\n            block_cnt <= 16'h0;\n        end else if (in_valid && out_ready) begin\n            if (block_cnt >= 16'd65530) begin\n                block_cnt <= 16'h0;\n            end else begin\n                block_cnt <= block_cnt + 16'd2;\n            end\n        end\n    end\n\n    assign am_insert = (block_cnt == 16'd65530) && in_valid && out_ready;\n\n    assign out_block0 = in_block0;\n    assign out_block1 = in_block1;\n    assign out_valid  = in_valid;\n    assign in_ready   = out_ready;\n\nendmodule\n```\n\n## 6. 与 lane_dist 的配合\n\n### 6.1 反压处理\n\n`eth_pcs_lane_dist` 模块接收 `am_insert=1` 后：\n\n1. 拉低 `out_ready`，反压传递到上游\n2. 在 2 个周期内输出 4 个 lane 的 AM\n3. 恢复 `out_ready`，继续正常数据分发\n\n### 6.2 时序示例\n\n```\n周期:        |  N    | N+1   | N+2   | N+3   | N+4   |\n             |       |       |       |       |       |\nblock_cnt:   | 65528 | 65530 |   0   |   2   |   4   |\n             |       |       |       |       |       |\nam_insert:   |   0   |   1   |   0   |   0   |   0   |\n             |       |       |       |       |       |\nout_ready:   |   1   |   1   |   0   |   0   |   1   |  ← lane_dist 反压\n             |       |       |       |       |       |\nin_block0:   | D0    | D2    | D2    | D2    | D4    |\nin_block1:   | D1    | D3    | D3    | D3    | D5    |\n             |       |       |       |       |       |\nlane_dist:   |       |       |       |       |       |\n  output:    | D0→L0 | D2→L0 | AM_L0 | AM_L2 | D4→L0 |\n             | D1→L1 | D3→L1 | AM_L1 | AM_L3 | D5→L1 |\n```\n\n## 7. 流水线\n\n本模块为直通模式，无流水线延迟。\n\n## 8. 数据流位置\n\n```\nTX: eth_pcs_64b66b_enc → eth_pcs_scrambler → eth_pcs_am_insert → eth_pcs_lane_dist\n```\n\n## 9. 参考文献\n\n- IEEE 802.3-2018 Clause 82.2.6 (Block Distribution)\n- IEEE 802.3-2018 Clause 82.2.7 (Alignment Marker Insertion)\n\n## 10. 修订历史\n\n| 版本 | 日期 | 描述 |\n|------|------|------|\n| 1.0 | 2026-04-10 | 初始版本 |\n| 1.1 | 2026-04-10 | 修正计数器为16-bit，计数范围0~65535 |\n| 1.2 | 2026-04-10 | 修正AM插入周期为16383（IEEE 802.3-2018），移除BIP计算（移至lane_dist） |\n"
}
```

**Output:**
```
Wrote file successfully.
